I'mma use Miley Cyrus as an example because I'm sure we all remember Wrecking Ball and that period of time. The writing had been on the wall but that was a very clear kinda snap in her career away from country-pop to WRECKING BALL. It left no questions as to what direction she was going in, and while I'm always a little worried when something like that does change because we know mental health is not a top priority in the entertainment industry, she came out the other side gaining popularity and getting to be her authentic self to her fans (presumably, I won't act like I personally know the woman).  This stunt from Jojo feels... forced to say the least. In what direction, I'm not sure. The obvious assumption is that she's faking this "edgy side" just for one album for publicity, then she'll go back to status quo after the hype dies down. The other side could be that she's being held back. I know from personal experience how difficult it can be to learn how to express your wants and needs and boundaries as a young adult, it can be near impossible if you have low self-esteem like me. This isn't to say Jojo siwa has low self-esteem, again I don't know her, but if she did then it might make sense that even though she WANTS to go with more mature music and aesthetics, she doesn't feel like she can stand up to the people around her who are using this as a publicity stunt and are corrupting the image Jojo actual wanted to go for. If the latter is what's happening, I feel really bad for Jojo... Bird in a cage...

This has led to TikTok going to war with JoJo Siwa, claiming she lied about writing the song. That she stole the song, etc.  The problem? She didn't do either of those things. She never claimed to be "scared while writing" Karma. She explicitly said she was scared of Karmaâ€”because its lyrics were outside her usual brand. She also didn't steal the song.
